        function OptanonWrapper() {
          const root = document.querySelector('#root');
          const cookieNotice = document.querySelector('#onetrust-banner-sdk');
          const acceptButton = document.querySelector('#onetrust-accept-btn-handler');
          cookieNotice.setAttribute("tabindex", "1");
          root.setAttribute("tabindex", "-1");
          const handleTab = (event) => {
            if (event.keyCode === 9) {
              root.focus();
            }
          };
          if (acceptButton) {
            acceptButton.addEventListener("keydown", handleTab);
            acceptButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
               setTimeout(() => {root.focus();}, 100);
            });
          }
        }

class="Nav__OpenMenuButton-sc-1hsi7ee-15 hNgzGt">Open<!-- --> submenu</button></li></ul></nav><div role="navigation" class="QuickLinks__Wrapper-sc-1pkxrvl-0 gXwfsO"><a href="/become-bfi-member" id="content-start"></div><main><div class="PageContainer__Wrapper-sc-jezgjv-0 fzVycg"><div class="HeroPage__BreadcrumbContainer-sc-e3utnp-5 ebdWFG"></div><div class="HeroPage__Outer-sc-e3utnp-0 dmiOmI without_image"><div class="HeroPage__Meta-sc-e3utnp-1 duZnlA page_meta"><h1 class="Headline__HeroH1-sc-e1fxl5-0 Headline__H1-sc-e1fxl5-1 kGnRqY gSyFTk" aria-label="">BFI privacy policy</h1></div></div><article class="PageContainer__MainContentWrapper-sc-jezgjv-1 fAeVDf child_page"><div class="slices__Slices-sc-1b0qhft-0 hVetDc"><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Your rights and how we use personal information.</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>The British Film Institute (the “<span class="caps">BFI</span>”, “we”) is a registered charity (number 287780), Royal Charter Body, National Lottery distributor and non-departmental public body funded by the department of Digital, Culture, Media and Sport.</p>
<p>The <span class="caps">BFI</span> is committed to respecting and protecting your personal information.</p>
<p>This policy seeks to inform you&nbsp;about:</p>
<ul><li>how and why we collect, process and store your personal&nbsp;information</li>
<li>your&nbsp;Rights</li>
</ul><p>This policy applies to all the <span class="caps">BFI</span>’s activities, services, products and platforms.</p>
<p>The <span class="caps">BFI</span> is the Data Controller and Richard Brousson is the Data Protection Officer under the <span class="caps">UK</span>’s Data Protection Act 2018 and the <span class="caps">EU</span>’s General Data Protection Regulation 2016.</p>
<p>All questions and complaints about the <span class="caps">BFI</span>’s use and handling of personal information should be addressed to <a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>.</p>
<p>You also have the right of complaint to the <span class="caps">UK</span>’s Supervisory Authority for Data – the Information Commissioners Office (the “<span class="caps">ICO</span>”). See <a href="https://ico.org.uk/make-a-complaint/">ico.org.uk/make-a-complaint</a>.</p>
<p>Information about personal data relating to volunteering, working for or applying to work for the <span class="caps">BFI</span> can be found here: <span class="caps">BFI</span> Privacy Notice: Workforce and&nbsp;Recruitment</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Information we may collect about you</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We may collect and process the following information about&nbsp;you:</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Information you give us</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><ul><li>Your prefix and name, billing and delivery address, postcode, email address, phone numbers, gender, date of birth, diversity monitoring information (anonymously unless stated otherwise), job title, personal identification documents, data relating to access or dietary requirements, payment card&nbsp;information</li>
<li>If you are making a grant application – your position within the company applying and relevant&nbsp;experience</li>
<li>If you are a student – your course details, relevant experience, school, college or&nbsp;university</li>
<li>You may provide us with this information when you set up an account (e.g. <span class="caps">BFI</span> Player, membership), apply for a grant (<span class="caps">BFI</span> Film Fund), apply for a course (<span class="caps">BFI</span> Education), apply to the <span class="caps">BFI</span>’s certification unit, buy tickets (<span class="caps">BFI</span> Southbank, <span class="caps">BFI</span> <span class="caps">IMAX</span>, <span class="caps">BFI</span> Festivals), fill in a form (competitions and surveys), complete an application form or otherwise apply for a job here either directly or via a third party, apply to volunteer, or correspond with us by phone, email or in&nbsp;writing</li>
</ul></div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Information we collect automatically</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><ul><li>Device <span class="caps">ID</span>s, <span class="caps">IP</span> addresses and other unique&nbsp;identifiers</li>
<li>Your activity on our services and platforms such as title selections and browsing&nbsp;history</li>
<li>Advertising identifiers, such as those on mobile devices, tablets and streaming media devices and information collected by cookies (please see our Cookies and internet advertising policy&nbsp;below)</li>
</ul></div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Information we collect about you from other sources</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><ul><li>Service providers that help us determine a location based on your <span class="caps">IP</span>&nbsp;address</li>
<li>Select partners that make our services available on their platform or with whom we offer co-branded services or engage in joint&nbsp;marketing</li>
<li>Publicly available information such as geo-demographic information and measures of capacity and propensity for giving to help us fundraise effectively and in line with our ethical policies from sites such as Companies&nbsp;House</li>
<li>Social media – depending on your settings you may have given us permission to access your personal information held by companies such as Facebook and&nbsp;Twitter</li>
</ul></div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Third parties may collect information about you</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>When using our websites and platforms third parties may collect information about you. This can be controlled by adjusting the settings in your internet browsers. There is more detail about adjusting your browser settings on the <a href="https://ico.org.uk/your-data-matters/online/cookies/">Information Commissioner’s Office&nbsp;website.</a></p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Why we collect and process your personal information</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We use your personal data for the following&nbsp;purposes:</p>
<ul><li>Carrying out research in the public&nbsp;interest</li>
<li>Maintaining, preserving and enhancing the <span class="caps">BFI</span> National&nbsp;Archive</li>
<li>Providing you with customer service when you visit, make use of or access any of the <span class="caps">BFI</span> premises, services or&nbsp;platforms</li>
<li>To administer any of your accounts, applications, contracts, enquiries or&nbsp;complaints</li>
<li>To process&nbsp;payments</li>
<li>Fulfil ticket, product, donation and membership&nbsp;requests</li>
<li>Contacting&nbsp;you</li>
<li>Providing you with information about things we think may interest&nbsp;you</li>
<li>To prevent, detect and investigate illegal activity such as fraud. The personal information we have collected from you will be shared with fraud prevention agencies who will use it to prevent fraud and money-laundering and to verify your identity. If fraud is detected, you could be refused certain services, finance, or employment. For further details of how your information will be used by us and these fraud prevention agencies, and your data protection rights, see <a href="https://www.cifas.org.uk/fpn">Fair Processing Notices for Cifas’s&nbsp;Databases</a></li>
<li>Analyse and understand our members, audiences and customers and improve our&nbsp;services</li>
<li>To protect and keep your personal information&nbsp;accurate</li>
<li>Using <span class="caps">CCTV</span> recording equipment in and around our premises for security&nbsp;purposes</li>
</ul></div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Special categories of personal information</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Data protection law recognises certain “special categories” of personal information, which include information revealing racial or ethnic origin, political opinions, religious or philosophical beliefs, trade union membership, genetic information, biometric information for uniquely identifying a person, information concerning health, and information concerning a person’s sex life or sexual orientation.</p>
<p>These special categories are considered particularly sensitive and so we will only collect and use this information where you have given us your explicit consent. For example, you may choose to tell us about your health condition before attending one of our events and we will only use this information for the particular event and not for any other&nbsp;purpose.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Lawful bases for processing your personal information</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Our legal basis for collecting and processing your personal information depends on the type of personal information and how we use it. There are 6 lawful&nbsp;bases:</p>
<ul><li>Consent – acquiring your agreement for us to process personal data for a precise purpose. You can withdraw consent for the storage and processing of data at any time (<a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>)</li>
<li>Public task – something we’re required to do as a public charity for example maintaining and enhancing the <span class="caps">BFI</span> National&nbsp;Archive</li>
<li>Legitimate interests – where we have a legitimate interest that isn’t overridden by your fundamental rights and freedoms for example something we think you’d be happy for us to do like contact you when you have actively shown an interest in our activities or&nbsp;services</li>
<li>Contract – fulfilment of a contract e.g. subscribing to <span class="caps">BFI</span> Player or becoming a <span class="caps">BFI</span>&nbsp;member</li>
<li>Legal obligation – where we have to use data as prescribed by&nbsp;law</li>
<li>Vital interests – protecting your health and personal&nbsp;safety</li>
</ul></div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Sharing of personal data</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We only share your personal data with third parties where we have a legal basis for doing so, such as with your consent or the fulfilment of a contract. For example, to invite you to an event and administer payments. We will never sell your personal&nbsp;information.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Transfers Outside of the European Economic Area (the “EEA”)</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Where we transfer personal information outside of the <span class="caps">EEA</span> for processing this is carried out in accordance with all applicable laws and with third parties we&nbsp;trust.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Retention Policies and Periods</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We only keep your personal information for as long as is necessary for the purpose for which it was collected. This depends on the personal information and the purpose for which it is processed. For precise information relating to the periods relating to each category of personal data, please contact <a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>. If you ask us to stop sending direct marketing communications to you, we will keep the minimum amount of information (e.g. name, address and email address) to ensure we adhere to such&nbsp;requests.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Security</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We use administrative, physical, managerial and technical measures to safeguard your personal information against loss, theft and unauthorised&nbsp;use.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Fundraising</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>The <span class="caps">BFI</span> will utilise your personal information to administer your relationship with the <span class="caps">BFI</span>. We may analyse your personal information to create a profile of your interests and preferences so that we can contact you with information relevant to you. We may make use of additional information about you, such as geo-demographic information and measures of capacity and propensity for giving from sites such as Companies House. This helps us understand the background of the people who support us so we can contact you in the most appropriate way, with the most relevant information; and helps us to make appropriate requests for gifts in line with our ethical policies. To change how we contact you or process your personal information (including if you would like us to stop doing so), simply email <a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Your Rights in Personal Information</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Your personal information is your data and you are in control of it. Where you have an account with us, you can access it and amend the data we hold and the marketing you wish to receive.</p>
<p>You can ask us to provide you with all the information that we hold about you, how we use it and why, utilising your right to be informed and your right to access. Contact <a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>.</p>
<p>You can then ask us to do the following with the personal information we hold about&nbsp;you:</p>
<ul><li>If it is incorrect, you can ask for it to be updated – your right to&nbsp;rectification</li>
<li>Restrict or object to it being processed at all or in a specific way — your right to restrict, right to object and right related to automated decision&nbsp;making</li>
<li>Ask for it to be deleted — your right to erasure, sometimes called the right to be&nbsp;forgotten</li>
<li>Ask for a digital copy of it – your right to digital&nbsp;portability</li>
</ul><p>Many of the rights listed above are limited to certain defined circumstances and we may not always be able to comply with your request. We will tell you if this is the case.</p>
<p>For more information on your rights in your personal information, please see the <a href="https://ico.org.uk/for-organisations/guide-to-data-protection/guide-to-the-general-data-protection-regulation-gdpr/individual-rights/"><span class="caps">ICO</span> guidance</a>.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Changes to this policy</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We will update this policy from time to time in response to changes to legal or regulatory requirements and changes in our activities, services or platforms. The date of the last update will be noted at the bottom of this&nbsp;policy.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Definitions </h2><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Personal Information, sometimes known as Personal Data</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Personal data means data which relate to a living individual who can be identified –</p>
<p>(a) from those data, or</p>
<p>(b) from those data and other information which is in the possession of, or is likely to come into the possession of, the data controller,</p>
<p>and includes any expression of opinion about the individual and any indication of the intentions of the data controller or any other person in respect of the&nbsp;individual.</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Data Controller</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Data Controller – An individual or an organisation which determines the purposes for which, and the manner in which, any personal data are to be&nbsp;processed</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Data Processor</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Data Processor – An individual or an organisation who processes personal data on behalf of the Data&nbsp;Controller</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Data Processing</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Data Processing – Anything you do with data: any operation, collection, recording, organisation, storage, adaption or disclosure of personal&nbsp;information</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">Data Protection Officer</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>The <span class="caps">BFI</span>’s Data Protection Officer, Richard Brousson (<a href="mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>), assists the <span class="caps">BFI</span> to monitor internal compliance, informs and advises on the <span class="caps">BFI</span>’s data protection obligations, and provides a contact point for data subjects and the <span class="caps">ICO</span>.</p>
</div><h2 class="Headline__H2-sc-e1fxl5-2 hwajTk" aria-label="">Cookies and Internet Advertising Policy</h2><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>We and approved third parties use cookies and other technologies, as well as advertising identifiers, for various reasons. For example, we use these technologies to make it easy to access our services by remembering you when you return, to provide and analyse our services. They are also used to learn more about you and your likely interests, and to deliver and tailor marketing or advertising. We want you to be informed about our use of these technologies, so this section explains the types of technologies we use, what they do and your choices regarding their&nbsp;use.</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">What are cookies?</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Cookies are small data files that are commonly stored on your device when you browse and use websites and online services. They are widely used to make websites work, or to work more efficiently, as well as to provide reporting information and assist with service or advertising&nbsp;personalisation.</p>
</div><h3 class="Headline__H3-sc-e1fxl5-3 bdTzLA" aria-label="">What are advertising identifiers?</h3><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><p>Advertising identifiers are similar to cookies and are found on many mobile devices and tablets (for example, the “Identifier for Advertisers” (or <span class="caps">IDFA</span>) on Apple iOS devices and the “Google Advertising <span class="caps">ID</span>” on Android devices), and certain streaming media devices. Like cookies, advertising identifiers are used to make online advertising more&nbsp;relevant.</p>
</div><div class="Text__Outer-sc-1acyvkb-0 cjbegI text_block"><h3><strong>Cookies and Internet&nbsp;Advertising&nbsp;Policy</strong></h3>
<p>The&nbsp;<span class="caps">BFI</span>&nbsp;and approved third parties use cookies and other technologies, as well as&nbsp;advertising&nbsp;identifiers:&nbsp;</p>
<ul><li>to make it easy to access our services by remembering you when&nbsp;you&nbsp;return</li>
<li>to provide and analyse&nbsp;our&nbsp;services</li>
<li>to learn more about you and your likely interests, and to deliver and tailor marketing or advertising that may be more relevant&nbsp;to&nbsp;you</li>
</ul><p>We want you to be informed about our use of these technologies. To find out more about the types of technologies we use, what they do and your choices regarding their&nbsp;use, please visit our&nbsp;<a href="/bfi-cookie-policy">Cookie policy&nbsp;page</a></p>
<p>
Updated April&nbsp;2022</p>

There are 6 lawful bases:</p>\n<ul><li>Consent – acquiring your agreement for us to process personal data for a precise purpose. You can withdraw consent for the storage and processing of data at any time (<a href=\"mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk\">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>)</li>\n<li>Public task – something we’re required to do as a public charity for example maintaining and enhancing the <span class=\"caps\">BFI</span> National Archive</li>\n<li>Legitimate interests – where we have a legitimate interest that isn’t overridden by your fundamental rights and freedoms for example something we think you’d be happy for us to do like contact you when you have actively shown an interest in our activities or services</li>\n<li>Contract – Contact <a href=\"mailto:dpo@bfi.org.uk\">dpo@bfi.org.uk</a>.</p>\n<p>You can then ask us to do the following with the personal information we hold about you:</p>\n<ul><li>If it is incorrect, you can ask for it to be updated – your right to rectification</li>\n<li>Restrict or object to it being processed at all or in a specific way — your right to restrict, right to object and right related to automated decision making</li>\n<li>Ask for it to be deleted — your right to erasure, sometimes called the right to be forgotten</li>\n<li>Ask for a digital copy of it – your right to digital portability</li>\n</ul><p>Many of the rights listed above are limited to certain defined circumstances and we may not always be able to comply with your request. We will tell you if this is the case.</p>\n<p>For more information on your rights in your personal information, please see the <a href=\"https://ico.org.uk/for-organisations/guide-to-data-protection/guide-to-the-general-data-protection-regulation-gdpr/individual-rights/\"><span class=\"caps\">ICO</span> guidance</a>.</p>\n"},"relationships":{"paragraph_type":{"data":null,"links":{"self":{"href":"https://core-cms.bfi.org.uk/api/slice/text-block/83487e50-448c-4e84-a783-86db3f934c84/relationships/paragraph_type?resourceVersion=id%3A495265"}}}}},{"type":"headline","id":"e1e90d36-37b6-49f6-95df-10413c9fb2c3","links":{"self":{"href":"https://core-cms.bfi.org.uk/api/slice/headline/e1e90d36-37b6-49f6-95df-10413c9fb2c3?resourceVersion=id%3A495266"}},"attributes":{"resourceVersion":495266,"published":true,"created":"2020-07-29T14:02:54+00:00","parent_field_name":"page_slices","hierarchy":"h2","title":"Changes to this policy"},"relationships":{"paragraph_type":{"data":null,"links":{"self":{"href":"https://core-cms.bfi.org.uk/api/slice/headline/e1e90d36-37b6-49f6-95df-10413c9fb2c3/relationships/paragraph_type?resourceVersion=id%3A495266"}}}}},{"type":"text-block","id":"1707b5ec-a6a5-4571-a89b-e942df104edc","links":{"self":{"href":"https://core-cms.bfi.org.uk/api/slice/text-block/1707b5ec-a6a5-4571-a89b-e942df104edc?resourceVersion=id%3A495267"}},"attributes":{"published":true,"created":"2020-07-29T14:03:08+00:00","parent_field_name":"page_slices","wysiwygEditor":"<p>We will update this policy from time to time in response to changes to legal or regulatory requirements and changes in our activities, services or platforms. They do not store any personally identifiable information.</p></div><div class="ot-desc-cntr ot-hide" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" id="ot-desc-id-C0002"><div class="ot-grp-hdr1"><h4 class="ot-cat-header">Analytics cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0002" id="ot-group-id-C0002" aria-checked="false" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0002" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0002"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0002"><span class="ot-switch-nob" aria-checked="false" role="switch"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Analytics cookies</span></label> </div><div class="ot-tgl-cntr"></div></div><p class="ot-grp-desc ot-category-desc">These cookies allow us to count visits to the site and tell us how you got to the site.
